 we had the powers of the spiritlands and my bloodstone at our fingertips and we would search every corner of the earth . 
 it was not impossible . 
 i nodded limply , grasping his hand as i allowed my mind to wander . 
 raquel 's jade green eyes filled my thoughts . 
 her little face always seemed so sad and that haunted me . 
 i wanted nothing more than to make her happy . 
 `` and i , too , '' cadmus agreed , reading my thoughts . 
 `` and we will . 
 once we get her back , she will be the happiest little girl in the world . 
 i will make sure of it . '' 
 he bent to kiss my forehead and i clung to him , inhaling his strength . 
 i would certainly need it on our quest . 
 one final journey . 
 it sounded so simple , like a last trip in an old car or a final visit to a store going out of business . 
 but it was n't the same . 
 our journey would not be simple . 
 i knew that already , even without using powers of prophecy . 
 there would be pitfalls and obstacles and challenges that i could n't even conceive of right now . 
 but i was stronger than i thought . 
 i had proven that to myself time and time again . 
 i was not weak ... i was the chosen one . 
 and as the chosen one , i knew that every journey since the beginning of time has always started with a single step . 
 i sighed and swung my legs out of bed . 
 the end
